   206‚Üí// ‚îÄ‚îÄ ObjectInstance ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
   207‚Üí
   208‚Üíclass ObjectInstance {
   209‚Üí  constructor(def) {
   210‚Üí    this.id        = def.id;
   211‚Üí    this.name      = def.name;
   212‚Üí    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   213‚Üí    this.position  = def.position;
   214‚Üí    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   215‚Üí    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
   216‚Üí    this.states    = def.states;
   217‚Üí    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
   218‚Üí    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
   219‚Üí    this.autoTimer = 0;
   220‚Üí    this._resetAutoTimer();
   221‚Üí  }
   222‚Üí
   223‚Üí  _resetAutoTimer() {
   224‚Üí    const s = this.states[this.state];
   225‚Üí    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   226‚Üí  }
   227‚Üí
   228‚Üí  /**
   229‚Üí   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   230‚Üí   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   231‚Üí   */
   232‚Üí  interact(action = 'use') {
   233‚Üí    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   234‚Üí    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   235‚Üí    if (!tr) return null;
   236‚Üí
   237‚Üí    this.state = tr.next;
   238‚Üí    this._resetAutoTimer();
   239‚Üí

## Project Structure

**Top-level directories:**
- `.git/` - Git repository
- `assets/` - Game assets (images, sprites, etc.)
- `docs/` - Documentation
- `scripts/` - Scripts
- `src/` - Source code
- `tools/` - Tools

**Top-level files:**
- `CAFE_SPEC.md` - Specification document
- `README.md` - Project readme
- `.gitignore` - Git ignore rules
- `.vercelignore` - Vercel ignore rules
- `index.html` - Main HTML entry point
- `vercel.json` - Vercel configuration

**src/ Directory Files:**
- `AIEngine.js` - AI engine for character behavior
- `Character.js` - Character class implementation
- `Engine.js` - Core engine
- `objects.js` - Interactive object state machines (8071 bytes)
- `scene.js` - Phaser scene
- `speechBubble.js` - Speech bubble UI component

### src/objects.js

```javascript
/**
 * objects.js ‚Äî interactive object state machines for the Japanese Home scene.
 *
 * Each object definition has:
 *   { id, name, position: { tx, ty }, interactMs, state, states }
 *
 * Each state can have:
 *   transitions: { use: { next: 'stateName' } }   ‚Äî triggered by interact()
 *   auto_next:   { state: 'stateName', after: N }  ‚Äî fires automatically after N seconds
 *   speech:      'string'                           ‚Äî shown as character speech bubble
 *   emoji:       'üç≥'                               ‚Äî floating emoji on transition
 */

// ‚îÄ‚îÄ Object definitions ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
// Japanese Home (912√ó642, 19√ó13 tiles, 48px each).
// Walkable interior: cols 1‚Äì17, rows 2‚Äì9.

export const OBJECT_DEFS = [
  {

    position: { tx: 3, ty: 3 },
    interactMs: 8000,

// ‚îÄ‚îÄ ObjectInstance ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ

class ObjectInstance {
  constructor(def) {
    this.id        = def.id;
    this.name      = def.name;
    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
    this.position  = def.position;
    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
    this.states    = def.states;
    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
    this.autoTimer = 0;
    this._resetAutoTimer();
  }

  _resetAutoTimer() {
    const s = this.states[this.state];
    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
  }

  /**
   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   */
  interact(action = 'use') {
    const s  = this.states[this.state];
    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
    if (!tr) return null;

    this.state = tr.next;
    this._resetAutoTimer();

    const ns = this.states[this.state];
    return {
      objectId: this.id,
      state:    this.state,
      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
    };
  }

  /**
   * Advance auto_next timers.
   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   */
  tick(deltaMs) {
    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;

    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;

    const s = this.states[this.state];
    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;

    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
    this._resetAutoTimer();

    const ns = this.states[this.state];
    return {
      objectId: this.id,
      state:    this.state,
      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
      auto:     true,
    };
  }
}

// ‚îÄ‚îÄ ObjectEngine ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ

export class ObjectEngine {
  constructor() {
    this._map = new Map(); // id ‚Üí ObjectInstance
  }

  addObjects(defs) {
    for (const def of defs) {
      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
    }
  }

  /**
   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   */
  tick(deltaMs) {
    const events = [];
    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
      if (ev) events.push(ev);
    }
    return events;
  }

  /**
   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   */
  interact(objectId, action = 'use') {
    return this._map.get(objectId)?.interact(action) ?? null;
  }

  getAll()   { return Array.from(this._map.values()); }
  getById(id) { return this._map.get(id) ?? null; }
}
```

## Summary

This is a Phaser 3-based game project called "AI Aquarium ‚Äî Maple's Caf√©". The main entry point is `index.html` which loads Phaser 3 from CDN and initializes a CafeScene at 912x642 pixels with pixelated rendering. The `objects.js` file contains an object state machine system for managing interactive elements (stove, fridge, tea set, kotatsu, TV, bookshelf, desk, bed, easel, bonsai) in a Japanese Home scene, with each object supporting interactive transitions, automatic state changes, speech bubbles, and emoji reactions.

    10‚Üífunction heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11‚Üí  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12‚Üí}
    13‚Üí
    14‚Üí/**
    15‚Üí * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16‚Üí * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17‚Üí * @param {number} cols
    18‚Üí * @param {number} rows
    19‚Üí * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20‚Üí */
    21‚Üífunction findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22‚Üí  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23‚Üí  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24‚Üí
    25‚Üí  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26‚Üí
    27‚Üí  const open = new Map();
    28‚Üí  const closed = new Set();
    29‚Üí
    30‚Üí  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31‚Üí  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32‚Üí
    33‚Üí  while (open.size > 0) {
    34‚Üí    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35‚Üí    let current = null;
    36‚Üí    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37‚Üí      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38‚Üí    }
    39‚Üí
    40‚Üí    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41‚Üí      // Reconstruct path
    42‚Üí      const path = [];
    43‚Üí      let node = current;
    44‚Üí      while (node.parent) {
    45‚Üí        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46‚Üí        node = node.parent;
    47‚Üí      }
    48‚Üí      return path;
    49‚Üí    }
    50‚Üí
    51‚Üí    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52‚Üí    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53‚Üí
    54‚Üí    const neighbors = [
    55‚Üí      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56‚Üí      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57‚Üí      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58‚Üí      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59‚Üí    ];
    60‚Üí
    61‚Üí    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62‚Üí      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63‚Üí      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64‚Üí      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65‚Üí
    66‚Üí      const g = current.g + 1;
    67‚Üí      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68‚Üí      if (existing) {
    69‚Üí        if (g < existing.g) {
    70‚Üí          existing.g = g;
    71‚Üí          existing.parent = current;
    72‚Üí        }
    73‚Üí      } else {
    74‚Üí        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75‚Üí          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76‚Üí          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77‚Üí          parent: current,
    78‚Üí        });
    79‚Üí      }
    80‚Üí    }
    81‚Üí  }
    82‚Üí
    83‚Üí  return null; // no path
    84‚Üí}

   139‚Üí    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20‚Äì40 s
   140‚Üí    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   141‚Üí    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   142‚Üí
   143‚Üí    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   144‚Üí    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   145‚Üí    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   146‚Üí
   147‚Üí    // Object interaction targeting ‚Äî set by engine, cleared on arrival
   148‚Üí    this.targetObjectId = null;
   149‚Üí    this.pendingAction  = null;
   150‚Üí  }
   151‚Üí
   152‚Üí  // ‚îÄ‚îÄ Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) ‚Äî feet at py) ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
   153‚Üí
   154‚Üí  get px() {
   155‚Üí    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   156‚Üí      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   157‚Üí    }
   158‚Üí    const next = this.path[0];
   159‚Üí    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   160‚Üí  }
   161‚Üí
   162‚Üí  get py() {
   163‚Üí    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   164‚Üí      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   165‚Üí    }
   166‚Üí    const next = this.path[0];
   167‚Üí    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   168‚Üí  }
   169‚Üí
   170‚Üí  // ‚îÄ‚îÄ Movement ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
   171‚Üí
   172‚Üí  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   173‚Üí    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   174‚Üí    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   175‚Üí    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   176‚Üí
   177‚Üí    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   178‚Üí      this.path         = path;
   179‚Üí      this.prevTx       = sx;
   180‚Üí      this.prevTy       = sy;
   181‚Üí      this.moveProgress = 0;
   182‚Üí      this.action       = 'walking';
   183‚Üí
   184‚Üí      // Set initial facing from first step
   185‚Üí      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   186‚Üí      this._playWalkAnim();
   187‚Üí      return true;
   188‚Üí    }
   189‚Üí    return false;
   190‚Üí  }
   191‚Üí
   192‚Üí  /** Convenience wrapper ‚Äî start interaction with a named object. */
   193‚Üí  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   194‚Üí    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   195‚Üí  }
   196‚Üí
   197‚Üí  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   198‚Üí    this.action         = 'interacting';
   199‚Üí    this.interactTarget = target;
   200‚Üí    this.interactTimer  = durationMs;
   201‚Üí    if (this.sprite) {
   202‚Üí      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   203‚Üí    }
   204‚Üí  }
   205‚Üí
   206‚Üí  // ‚îÄ‚îÄ Per-frame update ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
   207‚Üí
   208‚Üí  update(deltaMs) {
   209‚Üí    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   210‚Üí      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   211‚Üí      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   212‚Üí
   213‚Üí      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   214‚Üí      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   215‚Üí
   216‚Üí      // Advance tiles
   217‚Üí      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   218‚Üí        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   219‚Üí        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   220‚Üí        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   221‚Üí        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   222‚Üí        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   223‚Üí        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   224‚Üí      }
   225‚Üí
   226‚Üí      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   227‚Üí        this.moveProgress = 0;
   228‚Üí        this.action       = 'idle';
   229‚Üí        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   230‚Üí        this._playAnim('idle');
   231‚Üí      } else {
   232‚Üí        this._playWalkAnim();
   233‚Üí      }
   234‚Üí    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   235‚Üí      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   236‚Üí    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   237‚Üí      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   238‚Üí      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   239‚Üí        this.action        = 'idle';
   240‚Üí        this.interactTarget = null;
   241‚Üí        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   242‚Üí        this._playAnim('idle');
   243‚Üí      }
   244‚Üí    }
   245‚Üí
   246‚Üí    // Tick dialogue
   247‚Üí    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   248‚Üí      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   249‚Üí      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   250‚Üí    }
   251‚Üí
   252‚Üí    // Sync Phaser sprite
   253‚Üí    if (this.sprite) {
   254‚Üí      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   255‚Üí      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   256‚Üí    }
   257‚Üí
   258‚Üí    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   259‚Üí      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   260‚Üí    }
   261‚Üí  }
   262‚Üí
   263‚Üí  // ‚îÄ‚îÄ Perception ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
   264‚Üí
   265‚Üí  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   266‚Üí  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   267‚Üí    return objects.filter(obj => {
   268‚Üí      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   269‚Üí      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   270‚Üí      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   271‚Üí    });
   272‚Üí  }
   273‚Üí
   274‚Üí  // ‚îÄ‚îÄ Animation helpers ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
   275‚Üí
   276‚Üí  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   277‚Üí    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   278‚Üí    const next = this.path[0];
   279‚Üí    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   280‚Üí    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   281‚Üí    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   282‚Üí      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   283‚Üí    } else {
   284‚Üí      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   285‚Üí    }
   286‚Üí  }
   287‚Üí
   288‚Üí  _playAnim(type) {
   289‚Üí    if (!this.sprite) return;
   290‚Üí    const key = type === 'idle'
   291‚Üí      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   292‚Üí      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   293‚Üí    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   294‚Üí      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   295‚Üí    }
   296‚Üí    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   297‚Üí  }
   298‚Üí
   299‚Üí  _playWalkAnim() {
   300‚Üí    this._playAnim('walk');
   301‚Üí  }
   302‚Üí}

\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const GRID_COLS = 19;\n    const GRID_ROWS = 13;\n\n    function buildWalkableGrid() {\n      const grid = [];\n      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {\n        const r = [];\n        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {\n          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);\n        }\n        grid.push(r);\n      }\n      return grid;\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const CHARS_CONFIG = [\n      { name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6,  ty: 7,\n        dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?'] },\n      { name: 'Lucy',   label: 'Sol',   tx: 10, ty: 6,\n        dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'Such peaceful light...'] },\n      { name: 'Ash',    label: 'Nyx',   tx: 14, ty: 5,\n        dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect'] },\n    ];\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Engine setup \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();\n    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS });\n\n    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {\n      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({\n        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,\n      }));\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 UI state \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    let paused = false;\n    let speed  = 1;\n    let lastTs = null;\n\n    // Event log (newest-first)\n    const log = [];\n    const MAX_LOG = 150;\n    let logDirty = false;\n\n    // Track previous object states so we can log from\u2192to\n    const prevStateMap = new Map();\n    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Controls \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');\n    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n      paused = !paused;\n      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';\n      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);\n      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume\n    });\n\n    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {\n      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);\n        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));\n        btn.classList.add('active');\n      });\n    });\n\n    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {\n      // Reset object states to defaults\n      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {\n        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);\n        if (!obj) continue;\n        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';\n        obj._resetAutoTimer();\n        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);\n      }\n      // Reset sim clock\n      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;\n      // Clear log\n      log.length = 0;\n      logDirty = true;\n      // Update badge classes immediately\n      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n        updateObjectCard(obj);\n      }\n    });\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Helper: state badge class \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([\n      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',\n    ]);\n    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);\n\n    function badgeClass(state) {\n      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';\n      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';\n      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';\n      return 'other';\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Log helper \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {\n      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });\n      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;\n      logDirty = true;\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {\n      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);\n      if (!obj) return;\n      const from = obj.state;\n      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);\n      if (ev) {\n        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);\n        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);\n        updateObjectCard(obj);\n      }\n    };\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Build DOM cards (once) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    function initObjectCards() {\n      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');\n      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n        const card = document.createElement('div');\n        card.className = 'object-card';\n        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;\n        card.innerHTML = `\n          <div class=\"object-card-header\">\n            <span class=\"object-name\">${obj.name}</span>\n            <span class=\"state-badge\" id=\"badge-${obj.id}\"></span>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"position-hint\">tile (${obj.tx}, ${obj.ty})</div>\n          <div class=\"timer-bar\" id=\"timerbar-${obj.id}\" style=\"display:none\">\n            <div class=\"timer-fill\" id=\"timerfill-${obj.id}\" style=\"width:0%\"></div>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"timer-text\" id=\"timertext-${obj.id}\" style=\"display:none\"></div>\n          <div class=\"interactions\" id=\"int-${obj.id}\"></div>\n        `;\n        grid.appendChild(card);\n        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint\n      }\n    }\n\n    function updateObjectCard(obj) {\n      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);\n      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);\n      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);\n      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);\n      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);\n      if (!badge) return;\n\n      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;\n      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;\n\n      if (stateChanged) {\n        badge.textContent = obj.state;\n        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;\n        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;\n\n        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change\n        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});\n        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>\n          `<button onclick=\"window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')\">${a}</button>`\n        ).join('');\n      }\n\n      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)\n      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);\n      if (hasTimer) {\n        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;\n        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));\n        timerBar.style.display = '';\n        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;\n        timerText.style.display = '';\n        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;\n      } else {\n        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';\n        timerText.style.display = 'none';\n      }\n    }\n\n    function initCharacterCards() {\n      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');\n      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {\n        const card = document.createElement('div');\n        card.className = 'character-card';\n        card.id = `char-${i}`;\n        grid.appendChild(card);\n        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint\n      });\n    }\n\n    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {\n      const card = (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)\n        : char.targetObjectId\n          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)\n          : '\u2014';\n\n      card.innerHTML = `\n        <div class=\"character-name\">${char.label}</div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Action</span>\n          <span class=\"action-badge ${char.action}\">${char.action}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Position</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Facing</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${char.facing}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Target</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${targetName}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\" style=\"margin-top:4px\">\n          <span>Mood</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${char.mood}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"stat-bar\">\n          <div class=\"stat-fill mood\" style=\"width:${char.mood}%\"></div>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\" style=\"margin-top:4px\">\n          <span>Energy</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${char.energy}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"stat-bar\">\n          <div class=\"stat-fill energy\" style=\"width:${char.energy}%\"></div>\n        </div>\n      `;\n    }\n\n    function renderEventLog() {\n      if (!logDirty) return;\n      logDirty = false;\n\n      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');\n      if (log.length === 0) {\n        el.innerHTML = '<div style=\"color:#555;padding:4px 0\">No events yet.</div>';\n        return;\n      }\n      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => `\n        <div class=\"log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}\">\n          <span class=\"log-time\">${e.time}</span>\n          <span class=\"log-obj\">${e.objectId}</span>\n          <span class=\"log-transition\">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>\n          <span class=\"log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}\">${e.trigger}</span>\n        </div>\n      `).join('');\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Tick loop \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    function tick(ts) {\n      requestAnimationFrame(tick);\n\n      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {\n        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;\n\n        // Snapshot states before update\n        const snap = new Map();\n        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);\n\n        // Advance simulation\n        simEngine.update(realDelta);\n\n        // Detect auto-transitions\n        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {\n            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');\n            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);\n          }\n          updateObjectCard(obj);\n        }\n\n        // Update character cards\n        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));\n      }\n\n      lastTs = ts;\n\n      // Clock\n      document.getElementById('clock').textContent = simEngine.getSimTimeString();\n\n      // Event log (only when dirty)\n      renderEventLog();\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Init \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    initObjectCards();\n    initCharacterCards();\n    requestAnimationFrame(tick);\n  </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n"

\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const GRID_COLS = 19;\n    const GRID_ROWS = 13;\n\n    function buildWalkableGrid() {\n      const grid = [];\n      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {\n        const r = [];\n        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {\n          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);\n        }\n        grid.push(r);\n      }\n      return grid;\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Character definitions (mirrors scene.js) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const CHARS_CONFIG = [\n      { name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6,  ty: 7,\n        dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?'] },\n      { name: 'Lucy',   label: 'Sol',   tx: 10, ty: 6,\n        dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'Such peaceful light...'] },\n      { name: 'Ash',    label: 'Nyx',   tx: 14, ty: 5,\n        dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect'] },\n    ];\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Engine setup \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();\n    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS });\n\n    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {\n      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({\n        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,\n      }));\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 UI state \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    let paused = false;\n    let speed  = 1;\n    let lastTs = null;\n\n    // Event log (newest-first)\n    const log = [];\n    const MAX_LOG = 150;\n    let logDirty = false;\n\n    // Track previous object states so we can log from\u2192to\n    const prevStateMap = new Map();\n    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Controls \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');\n    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n      paused = !paused;\n      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';\n      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);\n      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume\n    });\n\n    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {\n      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);\n        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));\n        btn.classList.add('active');\n      });\n    });\n\n    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {\n      // Reset object states to defaults\n      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {\n        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);\n        if (!obj) continue;\n        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';\n        obj._resetAutoTimer();\n        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);\n      }\n      // Reset sim clock\n      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;\n      // Clear log\n      log.length = 0;\n      logDirty = true;\n      // Update badge classes immediately\n      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n        updateObjectCard(obj);\n      }\n    });\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Helper: state badge class \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([\n      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',\n    ]);\n    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);\n\n    function badgeClass(state) {\n      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';\n      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';\n      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';\n      return 'other';\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Log helper \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {\n      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });\n      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;\n      logDirty = true;\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {\n      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);\n      if (!obj) return;\n      const from = obj.state;\n      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);\n      if (ev) {\n        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);\n        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);\n        updateObjectCard(obj);\n      }\n    };\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Build DOM cards (once) \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    function initObjectCards() {\n      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');\n      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n        const card = document.createElement('div');\n        card.className = 'object-card';\n        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;\n        card.innerHTML = `\n          <div class=\"object-card-header\">\n            <span ${obj.ty})</div>\n          <div class=\"timer-bar\" id=\"timerbar-${obj.id}\" style=\"display:none\">\n            <div class=\"timer-fill\" id=\"timerfill-${obj.id}\" style=\"width:0%\"></div>\n          </div>\n          <div class=\"timer-text\" id=\"timertext-${obj.id}\" style=\"display:none\"></div>\n          <div class=\"interactions\" id=\"int-${obj.id}\"></div>\n        `;\n        grid.appendChild(card);\n        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint\n      }\n    }\n\n    function updateObjectCard(obj) {\n      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);\n      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);\n      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);\n      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);\n      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);\n      if (!badge) return;\n\n      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;\n      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;\n\n      if (stateChanged) {\n        badge.textContent = obj.state;\n        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;\n        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;\n\n        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change\n        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});\n        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>\n          `<button onclick=\"window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')\">${a}</button>`\n        ).join('');\n      }\n\n      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)\n      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);\n      if (hasTimer) {\n        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;\n        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));\n        timerBar.style.display = '';\n        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;\n        timerText.style.display = '';\n        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;\n      } else {\n        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';\n        timerText.style.display = 'none';\n      }\n    }\n\n    function initCharacterCards() {\n      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');\n      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {\n        const card = document.createElement('div');\n        card.className = 'character-card';\n        card.id = `char-${i}`;\n        grid.appendChild(card);\n        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint\n      });\n    }\n\n    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {\n      const card = (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)\n        : char.targetObjectId\n          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)\n          : '\u2014';\n\n      card.innerHTML = `\n        <div class=\"character-name\">${char.label}</div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Action</span>\n          <span class=\"action-badge ${char.action}\">${char.action}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Position</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Facing</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${char.facing}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\">\n          <span>Target</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${targetName}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\" style=\"margin-top:4px\">\n          <span>Mood</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${char.mood}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"stat-bar\">\n          <div class=\"stat-fill mood\" style=\"width:${char.mood}%\"></div>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"char-row\" style=\"margin-top:4px\">\n          <span>Energy</span>\n          <span class=\"char-value\">${char.energy}</span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"stat-bar\">\n          <div class=\"stat-fill energy\" style=\"width:${char.energy}%\"></div>\n        </div>\n      `;\n    }\n\n    function renderEventLog() {\n      if (!logDirty) return;\n      logDirty = false;\n\n      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');\n      if (log.length === 0) {\n        el.innerHTML = '<div style=\"color:#555;padding:4px 0\">No events yet.</div>';\n        return;\n      }\n      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => `\n        <div class=\"log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}\">\n          <span class=\"log-time\">${e.time}</span>\n          <span class=\"log-obj\">${e.objectId}</span>\n          <span class=\"log-transition\">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>\n          <span class=\"log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}\">${e.trigger}</span>\n        </div>\n      `).join('');\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Tick loop \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    function tick(ts) {\n      requestAnimationFrame(tick);\n\n      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {\n        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;\n\n        // Snapshot states before update\n        const snap = new Map();\n        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);\n\n        // Advance simulation\n        simEngine.update(realDelta);\n\n        // Detect auto-transitions\n        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {\n          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {\n            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');\n            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);\n          }\n          updateObjectCard(obj);\n        }\n\n        // Update character cards\n        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));\n      }\n\n      lastTs = ts;\n\n      // Clock\n      document.getElementById('clock').textContent = simEngine.getSimTimeString();\n\n      // Event log (only when dirty)\n      renderEventLog();\n    }\n\n    // \u2500\u2500 Init \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n    initObjectCards();\n    initCharacterCards();\n    requestAnimationFrame(tick);\n  </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n"

'./src/scene.js?v=15';\nnew Phaser.Game({\n  type: Phaser.AUTO,\n  width: 912, height: 642,\n  backgroundColor: '#1a1a2e',\n  scale: { mode: Phaser.Scale.FIT, autoCenter: Phaser.Scale.CENTER_BOTH },\n  render: { antialias: false, pixelArt: true },\n  scene: CafeScene,\n});\n</script>\n\n<!-- \u2500\u2500 Debug toggle button \u2500\u2500 -->\n<button id=\"debug-toggle\">Debug</button>\n\n<!-- \u2500\u2500 Debug overlay panel \u2500\u2500 -->\n<div id=\"debug-panel\">\n  <div id=\"debug-panel-header\">\n    <span>OBJECT STATES</span>\n    <span id=\"debug-clock\">\u2014</span>\n  </div>\n  <div id=\"debug-panel-body\">\n    <div id=\"dp-objects\"></div>\n  </div>\n  <div id=\"debug-panel-footer\">\n    <a href=\"debug.html\" target=\"_blank\">&#8599; Full dashboard</a>\n  </div>\n</div>\n\n<script>\n(function() {\n  const toggle  = document.getElementById('debug-toggle');\n  const panel   = document.getElementById('debug-panel');\n  const dpObjs  = document.getElementById('dp-objects');\n  const dpClock = document.getElementById('debug-clock');\n\n  let open = false;\n  let rafId = null;\n\n  const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([\n    'cooking','brewing','painting','working','tending','reading','on',\n  ]);\n  const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done','ready','open','cozy','resting']);\n\n  function badgeCls(state) {\n    if (state === 'idle')          return 'idle';\n    if (DONE_STATES.has(state))    return 'done';\n    if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state))  return 'active';\n    return 'other';\n  }\n\n  // Build DOM for each object row once, then update in place\n  let built = false;\n\n  function buildRows(objects) {\n    dpObjs.innerHTML = '';\n    for (const obj of objects) {\n      const row = document.createElement('div');\n      row.innerHTML = `\n        <div class=\"dp-obj\" id=\"dpo-${obj.id}\">\n          <span class=\"dp-obj-name\">${obj.name}</span>\n          <span class=\"dp-badge\" id=\"dpbadge-${obj.id}\"></span>\n          <span id=\"dptimer-${obj.id}\"></span>\n        </div>\n        <div class=\"dp-timer\" id=\"dptbar-${obj.id}\" style=\"display:none\">\n          <div class=\"dp-timer-fill\" id=\"dptfill-${obj.id}\" style=\"width:0%\"></div>\n        </div>\n      `;\n      dpObjs.appendChild(row);\n    }\n    built = true;\n  }\n\n  function updateRows(engine) {\n    const objects = engine.objectEngine.getAll();\n    if (!built) buildRows(objects);\n\n    dpClock.textContent = engine.getSimTimeString();\n\n    for (const obj of objects) {\n      const badge = document.getElementById(`dpbadge-${obj.id}`);\n      const tbar  = document.getElementById(`dptbar-${obj.id}`);\n      const tfill = document.getElementById(`dptfill-${obj.id}`);\n      const tspan = document.getElementById(`dptimer-${obj.id}`);\n      if (!badge) continue;\n\n      // Badge\n      if (badge.dataset.state !== obj.state) {\n        badge.textContent    = obj.state;\n        badge.className      = `dp-badge ${badgeCls(obj.state)}`;\n        badge.dataset.state  = obj.state;\n\n        // Rebuild use button\n        const existing = tspan.previousSibling;\n        // We rebuild via innerHTML of tspan for the button\n        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n        const actions  = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});\n        tspan.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>\n          `<button class=\"dp-btn\" onclick=\"window._dpInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')\">${a}</button>`\n        ).join('');\n      }\n\n      // Timer bar\n      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];\n      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);\n      if (hasTimer) {\n        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;\n        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));\n        tbar.style.display  = '';\n        tfill.style.width   = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;\n      } else {\n        tbar.style.display = 'none';\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  window._dpInteract = function(id, action) {\n    if (!window._gameEngine) return;\n    window._gameEngine.objectEngine.interact(id, action);\n  };\n\n  function renderLoop() {\n    if (!open) { rafId = null; return; }\n    if (window._gameEngine) updateRows(window._gameEngine);\n    rafId = requestAnimationFrame(renderLoop);\n  }\n\n  toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {\n    open = !open;\n    toggle.classList.toggle('open', open);\n    toggle.textContent = open ? 'Debug \u2715' : 'Debug';\n    panel.classList.toggle('visible', open);\n    if (open && !rafId) {\n      built = false; // rebuild rows on open in case engine wasn't ready before\n      rafId = requestAnimationFrame(renderLoop);\n    }\n  });\n})();\n</script>\n</body>\n</html>\n"

## Status DONE ## What Changed - **`debug.html`** (new): Standalone full-page dashboard with dark theme ‚Äî object cards grid (state badge, timer progress bar, Use buttons), 3 character cards (action/position/facing/target/mood/energy stat bars), scrollable event log with from‚Üíto transitions color-coded auto/interaction, Play/Pause/Speed/Reset controls, live sim clock. Imports `ObjectEngine`, `OBJECT_DEFS`, `SimulationEngine`, `Character` and runs a headless simulation (no sprites). - **`index.html`**: Added "Debug" toggle button (fixed top-right) that opens a 280px overlay panel showing live object states with state badges, timer progress bars, and Use buttons. Footer links to `debug.html`. Bumped scene cache-bust version to v15. - **`src/scene.js`**: Added `window._gameEngine = this.engine;` in `create()` so the overlay reads the actual running game state rather than a separate instance. ## Key Decisions - Overlay panel reads from `window._gameEngine` (live game engine) via polling rAF loop; interactions call `objectEngine.interact()` directly, affecting the actual Phaser simulation. - `debug.html` runs its own `SimulationEngine` + headless `Character` instances (null sprites work fine since `Character.update()` guards all sprite access), so it's fully independent from Phaser. - Used targeted DOM updates (not innerHTML rebuild per frame) so CSS `transition: width 0.1s ease-out` on timer fill bars works smoothly. ## PR / Branch - Pushed directly to `master` ‚Äî commit `3d3aa58`
